# gam

_PWG article — 127 sub-card(s), 627 sense(s) · RU 27/627 · EN 621/627_

## gam

`gam~~h0_00_pwg00`


**intro)** *gam*¦ (vgl. *gā*) bildet die Special-Tempora auf viererlei Weise: I. *gamati*
[NAIGH. 2,14.] *(ā) gamathas; gamātas, gamātha; (ā) gamet, gameyam* (
[P. 3,1,86], Sch.);
*(anu, nis) gamāni, (anu, ā) gamantu; gamam, gamat, gamāma, gaman*; med. *(sam) gamemahi, (sam) gamāmahai* . — II. *ganti*
[NAIGH. 2,14.] *(ā) gatha*
[ṚV. 8,20,6]; *(ā) gamyās*
[1,163,13.] *(ā) gamyāt; (ā) gahi, (ā) gantu, gantam, (ā) gantām, (ā) ganta* und *gantana*;
[2.] und 3. sg. *agan, aganma* (
[P. 8,2,65]), *agman; gan, gman* (aor. nach
[P. 2,4,80], Sch.);
partic. *gmant: adha gmantośanā* (Padap.: *gmantā) pṛcchate vāṃ kadarthā na ā gṛham . ā jagmathuḥ*
[ṚV. 10,22,6]; damit vgl. *adha gmantā nahuṣo havaṃ sūreḥ śrotā rājāno amṛtasya mandrāḥ*
[1,122,11.], wo aber
[ṚV. PRĀT. 8,15] und Padap. *gmanta* annehmen,
[SĀY.] *āgacchata* erklärt, ungeachtet der Betonung. Die Stelle ist dunkel und scheint verdorben zu sein. med. *aganmahi* . — III. *jaganti*
[NAIGH. 2,14.] *jagamyām, ˚yāt, ˚yātam, ˚yus; ajagan, ajaganta, ajagantana* . — IV. *gacchati* (nur diese Form in der klass. Literatur)
[DHĀTUP. 23,13.]
[P. 7,3,77.]
[VOP. 8,70.] — perf. *jagama, jagāma, jagantha* und *jagamitha, jagma, jagmathus* u. s. w.
[P. 6,4,98.]
[VOP. 8,96.] *jaganvaṃs* und *jagmivaṃs*
[P. 7,2,68.]
[VOP. 26,134.] [3,153.] *jagmuṣī*; fut. *gamiṣyati, gantā*
[P. 7,2,58]; aor. *agamat*
[3,1,55.] [6,4,98], Sch. ved. *ganta, gamema*, med. *˚agaṃsta* und *˚gata, ˚agaṃsmahi* und *˚agasmahi*
[P. 1,2,13]; prec. med. *˚gaṃsīṣṭa* und *˚gasīṣṭa* ebend., ved. *(sam) gmiṣīya* . — Das med., welches die Grammatiker vom simpl. nicht erwähnen, häufig im Epos, aber auch später, sogar in ungebundener Rede, z. B. *gacchamāna*
[PAÑCAT. 265,6.] — *gantum, gantave* (
[P. 3,4,9], Sch.),
*gantavai, gamadhyai; gatvāya* (
[P. 7,1,47], Sch.),
*gatvī, gatvā, ˚gamya* und *˚gatya*
[P. 6,4,38]; pass. *(ā) gāmi; gata*
[P. 6,4,37.]
- **EN:** *gam* (vgl. *gā*) forms the special tenses in four ways: I. *gamati* [NAIGH. 2,14.] *(ā) gamathas; gamātas, gamātha; (ā) gamet, gameyam* ([P. 3,1,86], Sch.); *(anu, nis) gamāni, (anu, ā) gamantu; gamam, gamat, gamāma, gaman*; med. *(sam) gamemahi, (sam) gamāmahai*. — II. *ganti* [NAIGH. 2,14.] *(ā) gatha* [ṚV. 8,20,6]; *(ā) gamyās* [1,163,13.] *(ā) gamyāt; (ā) gahi, (ā) gantu, gantam, (ā) gantām, (ā) ganta* and *gantana*; [2.] and 3. sg. *agan, aganma* ([P. 8,2,65]), *agman; gan, gman* (aor. after [P. 2,4,80], Sch.); partic. *gmant: adha gmantośanā* (Padap.: *gmantā) pṛcchate vāṃ kadarthā na ā gṛham . ā jagmathuḥ* [ṚV. 10,22,6]; with this vgl. *adha gmantā nahuṣo havaṃ sūreḥ śrotā rājāno amṛtasya mandrāḥ* [1,122,11.], where however [ṚV. PRĀT. 8,15] and Padap. *gmanta* assume, [SĀY.] *āgacchata* explains, regardless of the accentuation. The passage is obscure and appears to be corrupt. med. *aganmahi*. — III. *jaganti* [NAIGH. 2,14.] *jagamyām, ˚yāt, ˚yātam, ˚yus; ajagan, ajaganta, ajagantana*. — IV. *gacchati* (only this form in classical literature) [DHĀTUP. 23,13.] [P. 7,3,77.] [VOP. 8,70.] — perf. *jagama, jagāma, jagantha* and *jagamitha, jagma, jagmathus* u. s. w. [P. 6,4,98.] [VOP. 8,96.] *jaganvaṃs* and *jagmivaṃs* [P. 7,2,68.] [VOP. 26,134.] [3,153.] *jagmuṣī*; fut. *gamiṣyati, gantā* [P. 7,2,58]; aor. *agamat* [3,1,55.] [6,4,98], Sch. ved. *ganta, gamema*, med. *˚agaṃsta* and *˚gata, ˚agaṃsmahi* and *˚agasmahi* [P. 1,2,13]; prec. med. *˚gaṃsīṣṭa* and *˚gasīṣṭa* ebend., ved. *(sam) gmiṣīya*. — The med., which the grammarians do not mention for the simpl., frequent in the epic, but also later, even in unbound speech (prose), z. B. *gacchamāna* [PAÑCAT. 265,6.] — *gantum, gantave* ([P. 3,4,9], Sch.), *gantavai, gamadhyai; gatvāya* ([P. 7,1,47], Sch.), *gatvī, gatvā, ˚gamya* and *˚gatya* [P. 6,4,38]; pass. *(ā) gāmi; gata* [P. 6,4,37.]

**7)** — 7) vom partic. *upagata* erwähnen wir noch folgende Bedeutungen, welche sich oben nicht bequem einfügen liessen:
 a) angränzend, in der Nähe befindlich: *upagatā daśa yeṣām = upadaśāḥ* beinahe zehn
[VOP. 6,22.]
— b) heimgegangen, todt
[H. 374.]
— c) versehen mit (instr.): *hemnaivopagataṃ maṇim* in Gold gefasst
[MBH. 12,1545.] — caus. herbeikommen lassen: *enāmupagamayya*
[DAŚAK. 137,18.] — desid. zu wandeln begehren: *tasya mahānubhāvasyānupatham — kaḥ — upajigamiṣati*
[BHĀG. P. 5,24,26]; vgl. *upajigamiṣu* zu (acc.) — zu gehen wünschend
[MEGH. 43.]
- **EN:** — 7) of the partic. *upagata* we further note the following meanings, which could not conveniently be fitted in above:
a) bordering on, situated near: *upagatā daśa yeṣām = upadaśāḥ* nearly ten
[VOP. 6,22.]
— b) departed, dead
[H. 374.]
— c) provided with (instr.): *hemnaivopagataṃ maṇim* set in gold
[MBH. 12,1545.] — caus. to cause to come near: *enāmupagamayya*
[DAŚAK. 137,18.] — desid. desiring to wander: *tasya mahānubhāvasyānupatham — kaḥ — upajigamiṣati*
[BHĀG. P. 5,24,26]; vgl. *upajigamiṣu* to (acc.) — wishing to go
[MEGH. 43.]

**note)** — Vgl. *upaga, upagata* fgg., *upagāmin* und oben — *upā*, wohin die augmentirten Formen (durch * nach dem Citat bezeichnet) gleichfalls gestellt werden könnten, da z. B. *upāgamat* auch in *upa + ā + agamat* zerlegbar ist.
- **EN:** — Vgl. *upaga, upagata* fgg., *upagāmin* and above — *upā*, where the augmented forms (marked by * after the citation) could likewise be placed, since z. B. *upāgamat* can also be resolved into *upa + ā + agamat*.

**7a)** a) angränzend, in der Nähe befindlich: *upagatā daśa yeṣām = upadaśāḥ* beinahe zehn [VOP. 6,22.]

- **RU:** — 7) от partic. *upagata* укажем ещё следующие значения, которые выше не удалось удобно разместить:
 a) граничащий, находящийся вблизи: *upagatā daśa yeṣām = upadaśāḥ* почти десять
[VOP. 6,22.]
  <sub>DCS 600 · lexicographic</sub>

**7b)** b) heimgegangen, todt [H. 374.]

- **RU:** — b) ушедший домой, умерший
[H. 374.]
  <sub>DCS 600 · lexicographic</sub>

**7c)** c) versehen mit (instr.): *hemnaivopagataṃ maṇim* in Gold gefasst [MBH. 12,1545.]

- **RU:** — c) снабжённый (instr.): *hemnaivopagataṃ maṇim* вставленный в золото
[MBH. 12,1545.] — caus. заставлять приходить: *enāmupagamayya*
[DAŚAK. 137,18.] — desid. желать двигаться: *tasya mahānubhāvasyānupatham — kaḥ — upajigamiṣati*
[BHĀG. P. 5,24,26]; vgl. *upajigamiṣu* желающий отправиться к (acc.)
[MEGH. 43.]
— Vgl. *upaga, upagata* fgg., *upagāmin* и выше — *upā*, куда снабжённые аугментом формы (отмеченные * после цитаты) также могли бы быть отнесены, поскольку z. B. *upāgamat* разложимо и как *upa + ā + agamat*.

## abhyupagam

`gam~~h0_46_a_byupa`


**1)** — *abhyupa*
 1) herbeikommen, hinzugehen, zu Jmd treten, gehen zu, nach: *tatkṣaṇādevābhyupagamyādityaḥ provāca*
[PAÑCAT. 189,24.] *abhyupagata*

[SUŚR. 1,7,12.] *gurūnabhyupagacchati*
[MBH. 1,4847.] *asmānihāgatāneṣa niṣkramyābhyupagacchati*
[R. 3,18,24.] *(bhartari) paralokamabhyupagate*
[ŚIŚ. 9,13.] Jmd zu Hülfe kommen: *vayamabhyupagacchāmaḥ kṛṣṇeṇa tvāṃ pradharṣitam*
[HARIV. 2095.] zu Etwas schreiten: *tasmādabhyupagantavyaṃ yuddhāya*
[MBH. 14,327.] zu einem Zeitpunkt gelangen: *āṣāḍhīmabhyupagato bharataḥ*
[R. 4,27,11.] erlangen, erreichen: *atrābhyupagataḥ — vaidehyā iva darśanam*
[5,67,10.]
- **EN:** — *abhyupa*
 1) to come near, go up to, approach someone, go to, towards: *tatkṣaṇādevābhyupagamyādityaḥ provāca*
[PAÑCAT. 189,24.] *abhyupagata*

[SUŚR. 1,7,12.] *gurūnabhyupagacchati*
[MBH. 1,4847.] *asmānihāgatāneṣa niṣkramyābhyupagacchati*
[R. 3,18,24.] *(bhartari) paralokamabhyupagate*
[ŚIŚ. 9,13.] to come to someone's aid: *vayamabhyupagacchāmaḥ kṛṣṇeṇa tvāṃ pradharṣitam*
[HARIV. 2095.] to proceed to something: *tasmādabhyupagantavyaṃ yuddhāya*
[MBH. 14,327.] to reach a point in time: *āṣāḍhīmabhyupagato bharataḥ*
[R. 4,27,11.] to obtain, attain: *atrābhyupagataḥ — vaidehyā iva darśanam*
[5,67,10.]

**2)** — 2) sich für Etwas erklären, zugestehen, zugeben, einwilligen: *na tu dhanadāyāsāvabhyupagacchati*
[DAŚAK. 79,8.] *priyābhyupagate dyūte*
[MBH. 5,4239.] *taccāvaśyamabhyupagantavyam*
[KĀŚ.] zu [P. 1,2,55.] *svābhyupagatasyāvidyānṛtatvasya*
Sch. zu [KAP. 1,21.] *abhyupagataṃ tāvadasmābhirevam*
[ŚĀK. 69,22.] *tathā ca tenābhyupagate*
[DAŚAK. 201,8.] *abhyupagata = pratijñāta*
u. s. w. [H. 1489.]
- **EN:** — 2) to declare oneself in favour of something, concede, admit, consent: *na tu dhanadāyāsāvabhyupagacchati*
[DAŚAK. 79,8.] *priyābhyupagate dyūte*
[MBH. 5,4239.] *taccāvaśyamabhyupagantavyam*
[KĀŚ.] to [P. 1,2,55.] *svābhyupagatasyāvidyānṛtatvasya*
Sch. to [KAP. 1,21.] *abhyupagataṃ tāvadasmābhirevam*
[ŚĀK. 69,22.] *tathā ca tenābhyupagate*
[DAŚAK. 201,8.] *abhyupagata = pratijñāta*
u. s. w. [H. 1489.]

**caus)** — Vgl. *abhyupagama* . — caus. Jemand zur Einwilligung bewegen: *māmabhyupagamayya*
[DAŚAK. 82,5.] *etāvatkālaṃ tvaddāsa ityabhyupagamitaḥ*
[MIT. 268,13.]
- **EN:** — Vgl. *abhyupagama*. — caus. to move someone to consent: *māmabhyupagamayya*
[DAŚAK. 82,5.] *etāvatkālaṃ tvaddāsa ityabhyupagamitaḥ*
[MIT. 268,13.]

## samupagam

`gam~~h0_47_samupa`

- **EN:** — *samupa*

[MBH. 1,7718.] *saṃnikarṣaṃ me śīghraṃ samupagacchatu*
[R. 6,99,21.] *vasiṣṭhaṃ samupāgamat*
[MBH. 1,6673]*. [6872]*. [R. 1,18,9]*.

[KATHĀS. 5,122]*. *grahaṇam*
[R. 1,1,73].* — Die mit * bezeichneten Stellen könnten auch zu *samupā* gehören.
- **EN:** — 2) to enter into a state, a condition: *pañcatvaṃ samupāgamat*
[KATHĀS. 5,122]*. *grahaṇam*
[R. 1,1,73].* — The passages marked with * could also belong to *samupā*.

## samgam

`gam~~h3_08_sam`


**1)** — *sam*
- **EN:** — *sam*

**1.1)** 1)
Z. 14. fg. Die Stelle [N. 12,20] zu streichen, da hier *saṃgatyā* (von *saṃgati*) gemeint ist; auch
[MBH. 13,456] liest die [ed. Bomb.] richtig *saṃgatyā* . — desid. zusammenkommen wollen: *saṃjigaṃsate vatso mātrā*
[PAT. a. a. O. 6 (4),8,a.] gelangen wollen: *svargaṃ lokaṃ saṃjigāṃsat* ved. ebend.
- **EN:** 1)
Z. 14. fg. The passage [N. 12,20] is to be struck out, since here *saṃgatyā* (from *saṃgati*) is meant; also
[MBH. 13,456] reads the [ed. Bomb.] correctly *saṃgatyā* . — desid. "wishing to come together": *saṃjigaṃsate vatso mātrā*
[PAT. a. a. O. 6 (4),8,a.] "wishing to attain, reach": *svargaṃ lokaṃ saṃjigāṃsat* ved. ebend.

## gam

`gam~~h0_zz_pw00`


**root-header)** √*gam*¦, *ganti, gamati* ([NAIGH. 2,14]) und *gacchati* (nur dieses in der klass. Sprache); Act. und Med.
- **EN:** √*gam*¦, *ganti, gamati* ([NAIGH. 2,14]) and *gacchati* (only this in the klass. language); Act. and Med.

**1)** — 1〉 kommen.
- **EN:** — 1) to come.

**2)** — 2〉 kommen —, hingehen —, sich begeben nach, in, zu oder auf, gelangen nach oder zu, zu Theil werden; mit Acc. (auch mit *prati*), Loc. oder Dat.
- **EN:** — 2) to come —, to go to, to betake oneself to, into, towards or upon, to arrive at or reach, to fall to one's share; with Acc. (also with *prati*), Loc. or Dat.

**3)** — 3〉 zu einem Weibe (Acc.) gehen, so v. a. beiwohnen. *paśūn* mit Vieh Unzucht treiben. Ohne Object den Beischlaf vollziehen.
- **EN:** — 3) to go to a woman (Acc.), i.e. to have intercourse with her. v. a. to cohabit with. *paśūn* to commit bestiality with cattle. Without an object, to perform coitus.

**4)** — 4〉 in einen Zustand, eine Lage, ein Verhältniss (Acc.) kommen, gerathen; theilhaftig werden, erlangen; mit Acc. oder Loc. ([ṚV. 1,83,1. 86,3. 2,25,4. 7,32,10. 8,46,9]. [VĀLAKH. 3,5]).
- **EN:** — 4) to come, to fall into a state, a condition, a relationship (Acc.); to become partaker of, to attain; with Acc. or Loc. ([ṚV. 1,83,1. 86,3. 2,25,4. 7,32,10. 8,46,9]. [VĀLAKH. 3,5]).

**5)** — 5〉 aufbrechen, davon-, fortgehen. *ugrāya tapase* um strenge Kasteiungen zu üben [71,16].
- **EN:** — 5) to set out, to go away, to depart. *ugrāya tapase* in order to practise severe austerities [71,16].

**6)** — 6〉 hingehen, so v. a. sterben [176,6].
- **EN:** — 6) to pass away, i.e. v. a. to die [176,6].

**7)** — 7〉 verfliessen, vergehen, zu Ende gehen [NAIṢ. 7,109].
- **EN:** — 7) to elapse, to pass, to come to an end [NAIṢ. 7,109].

**8)** — 8〉 gehen, sich bewegen, wandeln; einen Gang oder Weg (Acc.) gehen. *jīvangacchati* so v. a. bleibt am Leben [57,2].
- **EN:** — 8) to go, to move, to walk; to walk a course or path (Acc.). *jīvangacchati* i.e. v. a. remains alive [57,2].

**9)** — 9〉 *manasā* in Gedanken sich begeben zu (Acc.); wahrnehmen.
- **EN:** — 9) *manasā* to betake oneself in thought to (Acc.); to perceive.

**10)** — 10〉 wahrnehmen, erkennen, errathen; Pass. verstanden werden, gemeint sein [227,20]. [234,1]. [237,26].
- **EN:** — 10) to perceive, to recognize, to guess; Pass. to be understood, to be meant [227,20]. [234,1]. [237,26].

**11)** — 11〉 *doṣeṇa* oder *doṣatas* Jmd (Acc.) beschuldigen, für den Schuldigen halten.
- **EN:** — 11) *doṣeṇa* or *doṣatas* to accuse someone (Acc.), to hold to be the guilty party.

**caus-header)** — Partic. *gata*
- **EN:** — Partic. *gata*

**ppp-header)** — 1〉 mit act. Bed.
- **EN:** — 1) with act. Bed.

- **EN:** — a) come. *evaṃ gate* since it has come to this, i.e. v. a. under these circumstances [43,16].

**ppp-b)** — b〉 gekommen zu oder in, gegangen nach oder zu, gelangt zu, übergegangen auf, Jmd zu Theil geworden, — gehörig, gerathen in. sich befinden auf, in, an oder bei, enthalten — ruhend in; die Ergänzung im Acc., Loc. oder im Comp. vorangehend. *kva tadgatam* so v. a. was ist daraus geworden? wie steht es damit? *hṛdgata* bis zum Herzen reichend [42,26].
- **EN:** — b) come to or into, gone to or towards, arrived at, passed over onto, fallen to someone's share, — belonging to, fallen into. situated on, in, at or by, contained in — resting in; the complement preceding in the Acc., Loc. or the Comp.. *kva tadgatam* i.e. v. a. what has become of it? how does it stand? *hṛdgata* reaching to the heart [42,26].
